<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маяться.html>ма́яться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">májatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изма́яться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suffer, to languish

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурь.html>ду́рью</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:маяться.html>ма́яться</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Xvátit dúrʹju <b>májatʹsja</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Stop fooling around!</span></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маять.html>ма́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">májatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***маячить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:маячить.html>мая́чить</a> (8749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Apparently from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маяк.html>мая́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maják</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lighthouse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маячить.html>мая́чить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">majáčitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to loom, to appear indistinctly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang around, to linger</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be in the offing, to loom ahead
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:маячить.html>мая́чит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:повышение.html>повыше́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">péred nim <b>majáčit</b> povyšénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in his case, a promotion is in the offing</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впереди.html>впереди́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:маячить.html>мая́чат</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́мены</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vperedí <b>majáčat</b> ekzámeny</i> ― <span class="e-translation">examinations are looming ahead</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">loom, appear indistinctly</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мелькать.html>мелька́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">melʹkátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">loom ahead, be expected</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предвидеться.html>предви́деться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">predvídetʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ожидаться.html>ожида́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ožidátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замаячить.html>замая́чить</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zamajáčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мгла.html>мгла</a> (6441)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mьgla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₃migʰleh₂</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mist, cloud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мгла.html>мгла</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mgla</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мгла.html>мглы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мгла.html>мглы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural missing</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>darkness</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">meteorology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mist, haze</li></ol>

***мгновение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мгновение.html>мгнове́ние</a> (1324)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мьгновениѥ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mĭgnovenije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mьgnovenьje</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mьgnǫti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to blink</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*migati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to blink</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мгновение.html>мгнове́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mgnovénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мгновение.html>мгнове́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мгновение.html>мгнове́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мгновение.html>мгнове́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>moment, instant, twinkling</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">meuble</i> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">mebel</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Möbel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мебель.html>ме́бель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mébelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мебель.html>ме́бели</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>furniture
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мебель.html>ме́бели</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razmeščénije <b>mébeli</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the placement of furniture</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***мегаполис.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мегаполис.html>мегапо́лис</a> (15088)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μέγας</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mégas</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">great, large, mighty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πόλις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pólis</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медведица.html>медве́дица</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">medvédica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медведица.html>медве́дицы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медведица.html>медве́дицы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медведица.html>медве́диц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>female bear; she-bear</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Ursa Major or Ursa Minor (see <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>Большая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:медведица.html>Медве́дица</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:малый.html>Ма́лая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:медведица.html>Медве́дица</a>)</li>
<li>tiger moth</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*medvědь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медведь.html>медве́дь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">medvédʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медведь.html>медве́дя</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медведь.html>медве́ди</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медведь.html>медве́дей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медведица.html>медве́дица</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bear</li>
<li>male bear</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bear (<i>of any bear-like animal</i>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bear (<i>on a stock market</i>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> large and clumsy person
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неуклюжий.html>неуклю́жий</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:медведь.html>медве́дь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">neukljúžij, kak <b>medvédʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">heavy-handed like a bear</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:медведь.html>медве́дь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xodítʹ, kak <b>medvédʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to walk ungracefully, like a bear</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:медведь.html>медве́дь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́хо</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наступить.html>наступи́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jemú medvédʹ na úxo nastupíl</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he's tone-deaf</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal  slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> safe <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медвежатник.html>медвежа́тник</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">medvežátnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***медвежатник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:медвежатник.html>медвежа́тник</a> (22655)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медвежатник.html>медвежа́тник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">medvežátnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медвежатник.html>медвежа́тника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медвежатник.html>медвежа́тники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медвежатник.html>медвежа́тников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bear-leader (synonym: <a href = vnd.unilang:вожак.html>вожа́к</a>)</li>
<li>bear hunter (synonym: охотник-медвежатник)</li>
<li>bear trainer (synonyms: дрессировщик-медвежатник; <a href = vnd.unilang:дрессировщик.html>дрессиро́вщик</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:медведь.html>медве́дей</a>)</li>
<li>bear dog</li>
<li>bear enclosure; bear cage (<i>or any place where bears are kept</i>)</li>
<li>broad double-edged knife</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> safecracker</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The term is mainly used in the slang sense (i.e., <i>safecracker</i>) nowadays.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медвежий.html>медве́жий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">medvéžij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мед.html>мед</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ве́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жий</b>
</p><p>Притяжательное <a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:медитация.html>медита́ция</a> (32165)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медитация.html>медита́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">meditácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медитация.html>медита́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медитация.html>медита́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медитация.html>медита́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>meditation</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ме<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ди.html>ди</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>та́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ци<span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a></b>

</p>

<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медлить.html>ме́длить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">médlitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помедлить.html>поме́длить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to delay, to linger, to procrastinate, to hesitate, to tarry</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медь.html>медь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">medʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медный.html>ме́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">médnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> copper; cupric, cuprous, cupreous</li>
<li>copper colored, reddish-yellow</li></ol>
